=== Min/Max


==== PMIN.B

===== Encoding

PMIN.B is encoded in the OP-32 major opcode with packed byte elements.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x6 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xc, attr: ['PMIN.B'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]

for i = 0 .. (XLEN/8 - 1):
    a = signed(s1[(8*i+7):(8*i)])
    b = signed(s2[(8*i+7):(8*i)])
    d[(8*i+7):(8*i)] = (a < b) ? a : b

X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

PMIN.B computes the signed minimum of corresponding packed 8-bit byte elements
of `rs1` and `rs2` and writes the packed byte results to `rd`.

==== PMIN.H

===== Encoding

PMIN.H is encoded in the OP-32 major opcode with packed halfword elements.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x6 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xc, attr: ['PMIN.H'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]

for i = 0 .. (XLEN/16 - 1):
    a = signed(s1[(16*i+15):(16*i)])
    b = signed(s2[(16*i+15):(16*i)])
    d[(16*i+15):(16*i)] = (a < b) ? a : b

X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

PMIN.H computes the signed minimum of corresponding packed 16-bit halfword
elements of `rs1` and `rs2` and writes the packed halfword results to `rd`.

==== PMIN.W

===== Encoding

PMIN.W is encoded in the OP-32 major opcode and is available only in RV64.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x6 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xc, attr: ['PMIN.W'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]

d[31:0]  = (signed(s1[31:0])  < signed(s2[31:0]))  ? s1[31:0]  : s2[31:0]
d[63:32] = (signed(s1[63:32]) < signed(s2[63:32])) ? s1[63:32] : s2[63:32]

X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

PMIN.W computes the signed minimum of corresponding packed 32-bit word elements
of `rs1` and `rs2` and writes the packed word results to `rd`. Available only
in RV64.

X[rd] = d

==== PMIN.DB

===== Encoding

PMIN.DB is encoded in the OP-IMM-32 major opcode using the double-wide
register-pair format. Available only in RV32.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 8, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rd_p' },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xe },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1_p' },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs2_p' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xc, attr: ['PMIN.DB'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
// Equivalent to two PMIN.B operations on even/odd register pairs
s1_lo = X[rs1_p * 2]
s1_hi = X[rs1_p * 2 + 1]
s2_lo = X[rs2_p * 2]
s2_hi = X[rs2_p * 2 + 1]

for i = 0 .. (XLEN/8 - 1):
    a = signed(s1_lo[(8*i+7):(8*i)])
    b = signed(s2_lo[(8*i+7):(8*i)])
    d_lo[(8*i+7):(8*i)] = (a < b) ? a : b

for i = 0 .. (XLEN/8 - 1):
    a = signed(s1_hi[(8*i+7):(8*i)])
    b = signed(s2_hi[(8*i+7):(8*i)])
    d_hi[(8*i+7):(8*i)] = (a < b) ? a : b

X[rd_p * 2]     = d_lo
X[rd_p * 2 + 1] = d_hi
----

===== Description

PMIN.DB performs packed signed 8-bit byte minimum on double-wide (register-pair)
operands. It is equivalent to two PMIN.B operations: one on the even registers
and one on the odd registers of each pair. All three operands (`rd_p`, `rs1_p`,
`rs2_p`) are register pairs and must specify even register numbers. Available
only in RV32.

==== PMIN.DH

===== Encoding

PMIN.DH is encoded in the OP-IMM-32 major opcode using the double-wide
register-pair format. Available only in RV32.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 8, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rd_p' },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xe },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1_p' },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs2_p' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xc, attr: ['PMIN.DH'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
// Equivalent to two PMIN.H operations on even/odd register pairs
s1_lo = X[rs1_p * 2]
s1_hi = X[rs1_p * 2 + 1]
s2_lo = X[rs2_p * 2]
s2_hi = X[rs2_p * 2 + 1]

for i = 0 .. (XLEN/16 - 1):
    a = signed(s1_lo[(16*i+15):(16*i)])
    b = signed(s2_lo[(16*i+15):(16*i)])
    d_lo[(16*i+15):(16*i)] = (a < b) ? a : b

for i = 0 .. (XLEN/16 - 1):
    a = signed(s1_hi[(16*i+15):(16*i)])
    b = signed(s2_hi[(16*i+15):(16*i)])
    d_hi[(16*i+15):(16*i)] = (a < b) ? a : b

X[rd_p * 2]     = d_lo
X[rd_p * 2 + 1] = d_hi
----

===== Description

PMIN.DH performs packed signed 16-bit halfword minimum on double-wide
(register-pair) operands. It is equivalent to two PMIN.H operations: one on the
even registers and one on the odd registers of each pair. All three operands
(`rd_p`, `rs1_p`, `rs2_p`) are register pairs and must specify even register
numbers. Available only in RV32.

==== PMIN.DW

===== Encoding

PMIN.DW is encoded in the OP-IMM-32 major opcode using the double-wide
register-pair format. Available only in RV32.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 8, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },

d_hi = (signed(s1_hi) < signed(s2_hi)) ? s1_hi : s2_hi

=== Comparison

==== PMSEQ.B

===== Encoding

PMSEQ.B is encoded in the OP-32 major opcode with packed byte elements.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x6 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0x8, attr: ['PMSEQ.B'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]

for i = 0 .. (XLEN/8 - 1):
    a = s1[(8*i+7):(8*i)]
    b = s2[(8*i+7):(8*i)]
    d[(8*i+7):(8*i)] = (a == b) ? 0xFF : 0x00

X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

PMSEQ.B (Packed Mask Set-if-Equal, Byte) compares corresponding packed 8-bit
byte elements of `rs1` and `rs2`. For each element position, if the elements
are equal the result byte is set to all ones (0xFF); otherwise it is set to
all zeros (0x00). The packed results are written to `rd`.

==== PMSEQ.H

===== Encoding

PMSEQ.H is encoded in the OP-32 major opcode with packed halfword elements.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x6 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0x8, attr: ['PMSEQ.H'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]

for i = 0 .. (XLEN/16 - 1):
    a = s1[(16*i+15):(16*i)]
    b = s2[(16*i+15):(16*i)]
    d[(16*i+15):(16*i)] = (a == b) ? 0xFFFF : 0x0000

X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

PMSEQ.H (Packed Mask Set-if-Equal, Halfword) compares corresponding packed
16-bit halfword elements of `rs1` and `rs2`. For each element position, if the
elements are equal the result halfword is set to all ones (0xFFFF); otherwise
it is set to all zeros (0x0000). The packed results are written to `rd`.

==== PMSEQ.W (RV64)

===== Encoding

PMSEQ.W is available only in RV64.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x6 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0x8, attr: ['PMSEQ.W'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]
d0 = (s1[31:0]  == s2[31:0])  ? 0xFFFFFFFF : 0x00000000
d1 = (s1[63:32] == s2[63:32]) ? 0xFFFFFFFF : 0x00000000
X[rd] = d1 @ d0
----

===== Description

The PMSEQ.W instruction compares corresponding packed 32-bit elements for
equality and produces a packed word mask in `rd`.

==== PMSLT.B

===== Encoding

PMSLT.B is encoded in the OP-32 major opcode with packed byte elements.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x6 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xa, attr: ['PMSLT.B'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]

for i = 0 .. (XLEN/8 - 1):
    a = signed(s1[(8*i+7):(8*i)])
    b = signed(s2[(8*i+7):(8*i)])
    d[(8*i+7):(8*i)] = (a < b) ? 0xFF : 0x00

X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

PMSLT.B performs a signed less-than comparison on corresponding packed 8-bit byte
elements of `rs1` and `rs2`. For each element, if the signed value of `rs1` is
less than the signed value of `rs2`, the corresponding byte in `rd` is set to
all-ones (0xFF); otherwise it is set to all-zeros (0x00).

==== PMSLT.H

===== Encoding

PMSLT.H is encoded in the OP-32 major opcode with packed halfword elements.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x6 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xa, attr: ['PMSLT.H'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]

for i = 0 .. (XLEN/16 - 1):
    a = signed(s1[(16*i+15):(16*i)])
    b = signed(s2[(16*i+15):(16*i)])
    d[(16*i+15):(16*i)] = (a < b) ? 0xFFFF : 0x0000

X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

PMSLT.H performs a signed less-than comparison on corresponding packed 16-bit
halfword elements of `rs1` and `rs2`. For each element, if the signed value of
`rs1` is less than the signed value of `rs2`, the corresponding halfword in `rd`
is set to all-ones (0xFFFF); otherwise it is set to all-zeros (0x0000).

==== PMSLT.W (RV64)

===== Encoding

PMSLT.W is available only in RV64.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x6 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xa, attr: ['PMSLT.W'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]
d0 = (s1[31:0]  <_s s2[31:0])  ? 0xFFFFFFFF : 0x00000000
d1 = (s1[63:32] <_s s2[63:32]) ? 0xFFFFFFFF : 0x00000000
X[rd] = d1 @ d0
----

===== Description

The PMSLT.W instruction performs signed less-than comparisons on corresponding
packed 32-bit elements and produces a packed word mask in `rd`.

==== PMSLTU.B

===== Encoding

PMSLTU.B is encoded in the OP-32 major opcode with packed byte elements.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x6 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xb, attr: ['PMSLTU.B'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]

for i = 0 .. (XLEN/8 - 1):
    a = unsigned(s1[(8*i+7):(8*i)])
    b = unsigned(s2[(8*i+7):(8*i)])
    d[(8*i+7):(8*i)] = (a < b) ? 0xFF : 0x00

X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

PMSLTU.B performs an unsigned less-than comparison on corresponding packed 8-bit

`rs1` is less than the unsigned value of `rs2`, the corresponding byte in `rd` is
set to all-ones (0xFF); otherwise it is set to all-zeros (0x00).

[wavedrom, ,svg]

{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x6 },

==== MSEQ (RV32)

===== Encoding

MSEQ is available only in RV32.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x6 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0x8, attr: ['MSEQ'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
X[rd] = (X[rs1] == X[rs2]) ? 0xFFFFFFFF : 0x00000000
----

===== Description

The MSEQ instruction sets `rd` to all ones if `rs1` equals `rs2`; otherwise it
sets `rd` to zero.

==== MSLT (RV32)

===== Encoding

MSLT is available only in RV32.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x6 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xa, attr: ['MSLT'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
X[rd] = (X[rs1] <_s X[rs2]) ? 0xFFFFFFFF : 0x00000000
----

===== Description

The MSLT instruction sets `rd` to all ones if `rs1` is less than `rs2` using
signed comparison; otherwise it sets `rd` to zero.

==== MSLTU (RV32)

===== Encoding

MSLTU is available only in RV32.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x6 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xb, attr: ['MSLTU'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
X[rd] = (X[rs1] <_u X[rs2]) ? 0xFFFFFFFF : 0x00000000
----

===== Description

The MSLTU instruction sets `rd` to all ones if `rs1` is less than `rs2` using
unsigned comparison; otherwise it sets `rd` to zero.


==== PMSEQ.DB

===== Encoding

PMSEQ.DB is encoded in the OP-IMM-32 major opcode using the double-wide
register-pair format. Available only in RV32.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 8, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rd_p' },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xe },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1_p' },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs2_p' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0x8, attr: ['PMSEQ.DB'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
// Equivalent to two PMSEQ.B operations on even/odd register pairs
s1_lo = X[rs1_p * 2]
s1_hi = X[rs1_p * 2 + 1]
s2_lo = X[rs2_p * 2]
s2_hi = X[rs2_p * 2 + 1]

for i = 0 .. (XLEN/8 - 1):
    a = s1_lo[(8*i+7):(8*i)]
    b = s2_lo[(8*i+7):(8*i)]
    d_lo[(8*i+7):(8*i)] = (a == b) ? 0xFF : 0x00

for i = 0 .. (XLEN/8 - 1):
    a = s1_hi[(8*i+7):(8*i)]
    b = s2_hi[(8*i+7):(8*i)]
    d_hi[(8*i+7):(8*i)] = (a == b) ? 0xFF : 0x00

X[rd_p * 2]     = d_lo
X[rd_p * 2 + 1] = d_hi
----

===== Description

PMSEQ.DB performs packed 8-bit byte mask-equality comparison on double-wide
(register-pair) operands. It is equivalent to two PMSEQ.B operations: one on the
even registers and one on the odd registers of each pair. All three operands
(`rd_p`, `rs1_p`, `rs2_p`) are register pairs and must specify even register
numbers. For each element, the result is all-ones (0xFF) if the elements are
equal, or all-zeros (0x00) otherwise. Available only in RV32.

==== PMSEQ.DH

===== Encoding

PMSEQ.DH is encoded in the OP-IMM-32 major opcode using the double-wide
register-pair format. Available only in RV32.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 8, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rd_p' },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xe },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1_p' },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs2_p' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0x8, attr: ['PMSEQ.DH'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
// Equivalent to two PMSEQ.H operations on even/odd register pairs
s1_lo = X[rs1_p * 2]
s1_hi = X[rs1_p * 2 + 1]
s2_lo = X[rs2_p * 2]
s2_hi = X[rs2_p * 2 + 1]

for i = 0 .. (XLEN/16 - 1):
    a = s1_lo[(16*i+15):(16*i)]
    b = s2_lo[(16*i+15):(16*i)]
    d_lo[(16*i+15):(16*i)] = (a == b) ? 0xFFFF : 0x0000

for i = 0 .. (XLEN/16 - 1):
    a = s1_hi[(16*i+15):(16*i)]
    b = s2_hi[(16*i+15):(16*i)]
    d_hi[(16*i+15):(16*i)] = (a == b) ? 0xFFFF : 0x0000

X[rd_p * 2]     = d_lo
X[rd_p * 2 + 1] = d_hi
----

===== Description

PMSEQ.DH performs packed 16-bit halfword mask-equality comparison on double-wide
(register-pair) operands. It is equivalent to two PMSEQ.H operations: one on the
even registers and one on the odd registers of each pair. All three operands
(`rd_p`, `rs1_p`, `rs2_p`) are register pairs and must specify even register
numbers. For each element, the result is all-ones (0xFFFF) if the elements are
equal, or all-zeros (0x0000) otherwise. Available only in RV32.

==== PMSEQ.DW

===== Encoding

PMSEQ.DW is encoded in the OP-IMM-32 major opcode using the double-wide
register-pair format. Available only in RV32.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 8, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rd_p' },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xe },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1_p' },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs2_p' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0x8, attr: ['PMSEQ.DW'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
// Equivalent to two MSEQ operations on even/odd register pairs
s1_lo = X[rs1_p * 2]
s1_hi = X[rs1_p * 2 + 1]
s2_lo = X[rs2_p * 2]
s2_hi = X[rs2_p * 2 + 1]

d_lo = (s1_lo == s2_lo) ? 0xFFFFFFFF : 0x00000000
d_hi = (s1_hi == s2_hi) ? 0xFFFFFFFF : 0x00000000

X[rd_p * 2]     = d_lo
X[rd_p * 2 + 1] = d_hi
----

===== Description

PMSEQ.DW performs 32-bit word mask-equality comparison on double-wide
(register-pair) operands. It is equivalent to two MSEQ operations: one on the
even registers and one on the odd registers of each pair. All three operands
(`rd_p`, `rs1_p`, `rs2_p`) are register pairs and must specify even register
numbers. For each element, the result is all-ones (0xFFFFFFFF) if the elements
are equal, or all-zeros (0x00000000) otherwise. Available only in RV32.

==== PMSLT.DB

===== Encoding

PMSLT.DB is encoded in the OP-IMM-32 major opcode using the double-wide
register-pair format. Available only in RV32.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 8, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rd_p' },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xe },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1_p' },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs2_p' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xa, attr: ['PMSLT.DB'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
// Equivalent to two PMSLT.B operations on even/odd register pairs
s1_lo = X[rs1_p * 2]
s1_hi = X[rs1_p * 2 + 1]
s2_lo = X[rs2_p * 2]
s2_hi = X[rs2_p * 2 + 1]

for i = 0 .. (XLEN/8 - 1):
    a = signed(s1_lo[(8*i+7):(8*i)])
    b = signed(s2_lo[(8*i+7):(8*i)])
    d_lo[(8*i+7):(8*i)] = (a < b) ? 0xFF : 0x00

    a = signed(s1_hi[(8*i+7):(8*i)])
    b = signed(s2_hi[(8*i+7):(8*i)])
    d_hi[(8*i+7):(8*i)] = (a < b) ? 0xFF : 0x00

X[rd_p * 2]     = d_lo
X[rd_p * 2 + 1] = d_hi
----

===== Description

PMSLT.DB performs packed 8-bit byte signed less-than mask comparison on
double-wide (register-pair) operands. It is equivalent to two PMSLT.B operations:
one on the even registers and one on the odd registers of each pair. All three

register numbers. For each element, the result is all-ones (0xFF) if the signed
`rs1` element is less than the signed `rs2` element, or all-zeros (0x00)
otherwise. Available only in RV32.

==== PMSLT.DH

==== PMSLT.DW

===== Encoding

PMSLT.DW is encoded in the OP-IMM-32 major opcode using the double-wide
register-pair format. Available only in RV32.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 8, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rd_p' },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xe },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1_p' },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs2_p' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xa, attr: ['PMSLT.DW'] },

[source,pseudocode]

s1_hi = X[rs1_p * 2 + 1]
s2_lo = X[rs2_p * 2]
s2_hi = X[rs2_p * 2 + 1]

d_lo = (signed(s1_lo) < signed(s2_lo)) ? 0xFFFFFFFF : 0x00000000
d_hi = (signed(s1_hi) < signed(s2_hi)) ? 0xFFFFFFFF : 0x00000000

X[rd_p * 2]     = d_lo
X[rd_p * 2 + 1] = d_hi
----

===== Description

PMSLT.DW performs 32-bit word signed less-than mask comparison on double-wide
(register-pair) operands. It is equivalent to two MSLT operations: one on the
even registers and one on the odd registers of each pair. All three operands
(`rd_p`, `rs1_p`, `rs2_p`) are register pairs and must specify even register
numbers. For each element, the result is all-ones (0xFFFFFFFF) if the signed
`rs1` element is less than the signed `rs2` element, or all-zeros (0x00000000)
otherwise. Available only in RV32.

==== PMSLTU.DH

===== Encoding

[wavedrom, ,svg]

    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1_p' },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },

    { bits: 2, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xb, attr: ['PMSLTU.DH'] },

[source,pseudocode]

// Equivalent to two PMSLTU.H operations on even/odd register pairs
s1_lo = X[rs1_p * 2]

s2_lo = X[rs2_p * 2]
s2_hi = X[rs2_p * 2 + 1]

for i = 0 .. (XLEN/16 - 1):
    a = unsigned(s1_lo[(16*i+15):(16*i)])
    b = unsigned(s2_lo[(16*i+15):(16*i)])
    d_lo[(16*i+15):(16*i)] = (a < b) ? 0xFFFF : 0x0000

for i = 0 .. (XLEN/16 - 1):
    a = unsigned(s1_hi[(16*i+15):(16*i)])
    b = unsigned(s2_hi[(16*i+15):(16*i)])
    d_hi[(16*i+15):(16*i)] = (a < b) ? 0xFFFF : 0x0000

X[rd_p * 2]     = d_lo
X[rd_p * 2 + 1] = d_hi
----

===== Description

PMSLTU.DH performs packed 16-bit halfword unsigned less-than mask comparison on
double-wide (register-pair) operands. It is equivalent to two PMSLTU.H
operations: one on the even registers and one on the odd registers of each pair.
All three operands (`rd_p`, `rs1_p`, `rs2_p`) are register pairs and must specify
even register numbers. For each element, the result is all-ones (0xFFFF) if the
unsigned `rs1` element is less than the unsigned `rs2` element, or all-zeros
(0x0000) otherwise. Available only in RV32.

==== PMSLTU.DW

===== Encoding

PMSLTU.DW is encoded in the OP-IMM-32 major opcode using the double-wide
register-pair format. Available only in RV32.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 8, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rd_p' },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xe },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1_p' },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs2_p' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xb, attr: ['PMSLTU.DW'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
// Equivalent to two MSLTU operations on even/odd register pairs
s1_lo = X[rs1_p * 2]
s1_hi = X[rs1_p * 2 + 1]
s2_lo = X[rs2_p * 2]
s2_hi = X[rs2_p * 2 + 1]

d_lo = (unsigned(s1_lo) < unsigned(s2_lo)) ? 0xFFFFFFFF : 0x00000000
d_hi = (unsigned(s1_hi) < unsigned(s2_hi)) ? 0xFFFFFFFF : 0x00000000

X[rd_p * 2]     = d_lo
X[rd_p * 2 + 1] = d_hi
----

===== Description

PMSLTU.DW performs 32-bit word unsigned less-than mask comparison on double-wide
(register-pair) operands. It is equivalent to two MSLTU operations: one on the
even registers and one on the odd registers of each pair. All three operands
(`rd_p`, `rs1_p`, `rs2_p`) are register pairs and must specify even register
numbers. For each element, the result is all-ones (0xFFFFFFFF) if the unsigned
`rs1` element is less than the unsigned `rs2` element, or all-zeros (0x00000000)
otherwise. Available only in RV32.

    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },

    { bits: 5, name: 0x1c },
]}

==== SATI (RV64)

===== Encoding

SATI is encoded in the OP-IMM-32 major opcode and is available only in RV64.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x4 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 7, name: 'w_uimm' },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x6, attr: ['SATI'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
n  = w_uimm[5:0]

minval = 0xFFFF_FFFF_FFFF_FFFF << n
maxval = ~minval

if (s1 <_s minval):
    vxsat = 1
    X[rd] = minval
else if (s1 >_s maxval):
    vxsat = 1
    X[rd] = maxval
else:
    X[rd] = s1
----

===== Description

The SATI instruction saturates `rs1` to a signed range determined by the
immediate `n` and writes the result to `rd`.

===== Notes

* `vxsat` is set to 1 if saturation occurs.

==== USATI (RV64)

===== Encoding

USATI is encoded in the OP-IMM-32 major opcode and is available only in RV64.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x4 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 7, name: 'w_uimm' },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2, attr: ['USATI'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
n  = w_uimm[5:0]

maxval = ~(0xFFFF_FFFF_FFFF_FFFF << n)

if (s1 <_s 0):
    vxsat = 1
    X[rd] = 0
else if (s1 >_s maxval):
    vxsat = 1
    X[rd] = maxval
else:
    X[rd] = s1
----

===== Description

The USATI instruction saturates `rs1` to the unsigned range [0, maxval]
determined by the immediate `n` and writes the result to `rd`.

===== Notes

* `vxsat` is set to 1 if saturation occurs.

=== Shift Operations

==== PSLL.BS

===== Encoding

PSLL.BS is encoded in the OP-IMM-32 major opcode.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x0, attr: ['PSLL.BS'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1    = X[rs1]
shamt = X[rs2][4:0]
for i = 0 .. (XLEN/8 - 1):
    b = s1[(8*i+7):(8*i)]
    d[(8*i+7):(8*i)] = (zero_extend(32, b) << shamt)[7:0]
X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

The PSLL.BS instruction shifts each packed 8-bit element of `rs1` left by the
shift amount in `rs2[4:0]` and writes the packed byte result to `rd`.

==== PSLL.HS

===== Encoding

PSLL.HS is encoded in the OP-IMM-32 major opcode.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x0, attr: ['PSLL.HS'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1    = X[rs1]
shamt = X[rs2][4:0]
for i = 0 .. (XLEN/16 - 1):

    d[(16*i+15):(16*i)] = (zero_extend(32, h) << shamt)[15:0]
X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

The PSLL.HS instruction shifts each packed 16-bit element of `rs1` left by the
shift amount in `rs2[4:0]` and writes the packed halfword result to `rd`.

=== Saturating/Rounding Shift

==== PSSHA.HS

===== Encoding

PSSHA.HS is encoded in the OP-IMM-32 major opcode.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x6, attr: ['PSSHA.HS'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1    = X[rs1]
shamt = X[rs2][7:0]
sshamt = signed(shamt)

for i = 0 .. (XLEN/16 - 1):
    h  = s1[(16*i+15):(16*i)]
    xh = sign_extend(32, h)

    if sshamt < 0:
        // arithmetic shift right by (-sshamt), saturating not required
        if sshamt <= -16:
            r = xh[31:16]
        else
            r = (xh >> (0 - shamt)[3:0])[15:0]
    else:
        // shift left with signed saturation to 16-bit range
        if sshamt >= 16:
            shx = (h @ 0x0000)
        else
            shx = xh << shamt[3:0]

        if shx <_s 0xFFFF8000:
            vxsat = 1
            r = 0x8000
        else if shx >_s 0x00007FFF:
            vxsat = 1
            r = 0x7FFF
        else
            r = shx[15:0]

    d[(16*i+15):(16*i)] = r

X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

The PSSHA.HS instruction performs a signed variable shift on each packed 16-bit
element of `rs1` using the signed shift amount in `rs2[7:0]`. Left shifts saturate
to the signed 16-bit range.

===== Notes

* `vxsat` is set to 1 if saturation occurs in any element.

==== PSSHA.WS (RV64)

===== Encoding

PSSHA.WS is available only in RV64.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x6, attr: ['PSSHA.WS'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation
// (use your Sail-derived pseudocode as previously, unchanged)

===== Description

The PSSHA.WS instruction performs a signed variable shift on each packed 32-bit
element of `rs1` using the signed shift amount in `rs2[7:0]`. Left shifts
saturate to the signed 32-bit range.

==== PSSHAR.HS

===== Encoding

PSSHAR.HS is encoded in the OP-IMM-32 major opcode.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x7, attr: ['PSSHAR.HS'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1     = X[rs1]
shamt  = X[rs2][7:0]
sshamt = signed(shamt)

for i = 0 .. (XLEN/16 - 1):
    h = s1[(16*i+15):(16*i)]    // signed 16-bit

    if sshamt < 0:
        // arithmetic right shift with rounding
        x  = sign_extend(32, h) @ 0b0          // 33-bit
        y  = (sshamt <= -16) ? x[32:16]
                             : (x >> (0 - shamt)[3:0])[16:0]
        r  = (y + 1)[16:1]
    else:
        // shift left with signed saturation to 16-bit range
        shx = (sshamt >= 16) ? (h @ 0x0000)
                             : (sign_extend(32, h) << shamt[3:0])

        if shx <_s 0xFFFF8000:
            vxsat = 1
            r = 0x8000
        else if shx >_s 0x00007FFF:
            vxsat = 1
            r = 0x7FFF
        else
            r = shx[15:0]

    d[(16*i+15):(16*i)] = r

X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

The PSSHAR.HS instruction performs a signed variable shift on each packed 16-bit
element of `rs1` using the signed shift amount in `rs2[7:0]`. Right shifts are
rounded, and left shifts saturate to the signed 16-bit range.

===== Notes

* `vxsat` is set to 1 if saturation occurs in any element.

==== PSSHAR.WS (RV64)

===== Encoding

PSSHAR.WS is available only in RV64.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x7, attr: ['PSSHAR.WS'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation
// (use your Sail-derived pseudocode as previously, unchanged)

===== Description

The PSSHAR.WS instruction performs a signed variable shift on each packed 32-bit
element of `rs1` using the signed shift amount in `rs2[7:0]`. Right shifts are
rounded, and left shifts saturate to the signed 32-bit range.

==== SSHA (RV32)

===== Encoding

SSHA is encoded in the OP-IMM-32 major opcode and is available only in RV32.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x6, attr: ['SSHA'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1     = X[rs1]
shamt  = X[rs2][7:0]
sshamt = signed(shamt)
xs1    = sign_extend(64, s1)

if sshamt < 0:
    if sshamt <= -32:
        X[rd] = xs1[63:32]
    else
        X[rd] = (xs1 >> (0 - shamt)[4:0])[31:0]
else:
    shx = (sshamt >= 32) ? (s1 @ 0x00000000)
                         : (xs1 << shamt[4:0])

    if shx <_s 0xFFFFFFFF80000000:
        vxsat = 1
        X[rd] = 0x80000000
    else if shx >_s 0x000000007FFFFFFF:
        vxsat = 1
        X[rd] = 0x7FFFFFFF
    else
        X[rd] = shx[31:0]
----

===== Description

The SSHA instruction performs a signed variable shift of `rs1` using the signed
shift amount in `rs2[7:0]`. Left shifts saturate to the signed 32-bit range.

==== SSHAR (RV32)

===== Encoding

SSHAR is encoded in the OP-IMM-32 major opcode and is available only in RV32.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x7, attr: ['SSHAR'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1     = X[rs1]
shamt  = X[rs2][7:0]
sshamt = signed(shamt)

if sshamt < 0:
    // arithmetic right shift with rounding
    x  = sign_extend(64, s1) @ 0b0            // 65-bit
    y  = (sshamt <= -32) ? x[64:32]
                         : (x >> (0 - shamt)[4:0])[32:0]
    X[rd] = (y + 1)[32:1]
else:
    // shift left with signed saturation to 32-bit range
    shx = (sshamt >= 32) ? (s1 @ 0x00000000)
                         : (sign_extend(64, s1) << shamt[4:0])

    if shx <_s 0xFFFFFFFF80000000:
        vxsat = 1
        X[rd] = 0x80000000
    else if shx >_s 0x000000007FFFFFFF:
        vxsat = 1
        X[rd] = 0x7FFFFFFF
    else
        X[rd] = shx[31:0]
----

===== Description

The SSHAR instruction performs a signed variable shift of `rs1` using the signed
shift amount in `rs2[7:0]`. Right shifts are rounded, and left shifts saturate
to the signed 32-bit range.

===== Notes

* `vxsat` is set to 1 if saturation occurs.

==== SSLAI

==== SHA (RV64)

===== Encoding

SHA is encoded in the OP-32 major opcode and is available only in RV64.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x3 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x6, attr: ['SHA'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1     = X[rs1]
shamt  = X[rs2][7:0]
sshamt = signed(shamt)

if (sshamt < 0):
    xs1 = sign_extend(128, s1)
    if (sshamt <= -64):
        X[rd] = xs1[127:64]
    else:
        X[rd] = (xs1 >> (0 - shamt)[5:0])[63:0]
else:
    if (sshamt >= 64):
        X[rd] = 0
    else:
        X[rd] = s1 << shamt[5:0]
----

===== Description

The SHA instruction performs a signed variable shift of `rs1` using the signed
shift amount in `rs2[7:0]`. Negative shift amounts shift right; non-negative
shift amounts shift left.

==== SHAR (RV64)

===== Encoding

SHAR is encoded in the OP-32 major opcode and is available only in RV64.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x3 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x7, attr: ['SHAR'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1     = X[rs1]
shamt  = X[rs2][7:0]
sshamt = signed(shamt)

if (sshamt < 0):
    xs1 = sign_extend(128, s1) @ 0b0          // 129-bit
    if (sshamt <= -64):
        shx = xs1[128:64]
    else:
        shx = (xs1 >> (0 - shamt)[5:0])[64:0]
    X[rd] = (shx + 1)[64:1]
else:
    if (sshamt >= 64):
        X[rd] = 0
    else:
        X[rd] = s1 << shamt[5:0]
----

===== Description

The SHAR instruction matches SHA for non-negative shift amounts. For negative
shift amounts it performs a rounding right shift as specified in the Sail code.

=== Pair Operations

==== PPAIRE.B

===== Encoding

PPAIRE.B is encoded in the OP-32 major opcode with packed-byte pairing. :contentReference[oaicite:0]{index=0}

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x4 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x0, attr: ['PPAIRE.B'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]

for i = 0 .. (XLEN/16 - 1):
    a = s1[(16*i+15):(16*i)]
    b = s2[(16*i+15):(16*i)]
    d[(16*i+15):(16*i)] = b[7:0] @ a[7:0]

X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

The PPAIRE.B instruction forms packed 16-bit elements by pairing the low byte of each
halfword element of `rs2` as the high byte with the low byte of the corresponding
halfword element of `rs1` as the low byte.

[wavedrom, ,svg]

{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },

    { bits: 3, name: 0x4 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x1, attr: ['PPAIREO.B'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]

X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

The PPAIREO.B instruction pairs the high byte of each halfword element of `rs2` with
the low byte of the corresponding halfword element of `rs1`, producing packed halfwords.

=== Zip/Unzip and Byte-Reverse

==== ZIP8P (RV64)

===== Encoding

ZIP8P is encoded in the OP-32 major opcode and is available only in RV64. :contentReference[oaicite:5]{index=5}

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x7, attr: ['ZIP8P'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]

X[rd] =
    s2[31:24] @ s1[31:24] @ s2[23:16] @ s1[23:16]
  @ s2[15:8]  @ s1[15:8]  @ s2[7:0]   @ s1[7:0]
----

===== Description

The ZIP8P instruction interleaves bytes from `rs2` and `rs1` to form a packed 64-bit result:
for each byte position, the corresponding byte from `rs2` is placed above the byte from `rs1`.

==== ZIP8HP (RV64)

===== Encoding

ZIP8HP is encoded in the OP-32 major opcode and is available only in RV64. :contentReference[oaicite:1]{index=1}

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x7, attr: ['ZIP8HP'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]

X[rd] =
    s2[63:56] @ s1[63:56] @ s2[55:48] @ s1[55:48]
  @ s2[47:40] @ s1[47:40] @ s2[39:32] @ s1[39:32]
----

===== Description

The ZIP8HP instruction interleaves bytes from the high 32-bit halves of `rs2` and
`rs1` to form a 64-bit result.

==== UNZIP8P (RV64)

===== Encoding

UNZIP8P is encoded in the OP-32 major opcode and is available only in RV64. :contentReference[oaicite:2]{index=2}

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x6, attr: ['UNZIP8P'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]

X[rd] =
    s2[55:48] @ s2[39:32] @ s2[23:16] @ s2[7:0]
  @ s1[55:48] @ s1[39:32] @ s1[23:16] @ s1[7:0]
----

===== Description

The UNZIP8P instruction de-interleaves bytes from `rs2` and `rs1` to form a 64-bit
result containing selected byte lanes from each source.

==== UNZIP8HP (RV64)

===== Encoding

UNZIP8HP is encoded in the OP-32 major opcode and is available only in RV64. :contentReference[oaicite:3]{index=3}

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x6, attr: ['UNZIP8HP'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]

X[rd] =
    s2[63:56] @ s2[47:40] @ s2[31:24] @ s2[15:8]
  @ s1[63:56] @ s1[47:40] @ s1[31:24] @ s1[15:8]
----

===== Description

The UNZIP8HP instruction de-interleaves bytes from `rs2` and `rs1` using the
high-part byte selection pattern and forms a 64-bit result.

==== ZIP16P (RV64)

==== REV16 (RV64)

===== Encoding

REV16 is a scalar instruction encoded in the OP-IMM major opcode and is available only in RV64. :contentReference[oaicite:4]{index=4}

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x13 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x5 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 12, name: 0x6b0 },
]}
....

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
X[rd] = s1[15:0] @ s1[31:16] @ s1[47:32] @ s1[63:48]
----

===== Description

The REV16 instruction reverses the order of 16-bit chunks within the 64-bit value in `rs1`.

=== Miscellaneous Scalar

==== ABS

===== Encoding

ABS is encoded in the OP-IMM major opcode.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x13 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 12, name: 'imm=0x607' },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
X[rd] = (signed(s1) < 0) ? (0 - s1) : s1
----

===== Description

ABS writes the absolute value of `X[rs1]` to `rd`.

==== ABSW (RV64)

===== Encoding

ABSW is encoded in the OP-IMM-32 major opcode and is available only in RV64.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 12, name: 'imm=0x607' },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
w = X[rs1][31:0]
X[rd] = sign_extend(64, (signed(w) <_s 0) ? (0 - w) : w)
----

===== Description

ABSW writes the absolute value of the low 32 bits of `rs1` (treated as signed)
to `rd`, sign-extended to XLEN.

==== CLS

===== Encoding

CLS is encoded in the OP-IMM major opcode.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x13 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 12, name: 'imm=0x603' },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
v = X[rs1]
lo_bound = to_bits(XLEN, -(2^(XLEN - 2)))
hi_bound = ~lo_bound
c = 0

while (c < XLEN - 1) & (v >=_s lo_bound) & (v <=_s hi_bound) do
    c = c + 1
    v = v << 1

X[rd] = to_bits(XLEN, c)
----

===== Description

CLS returns the count `c` produced by the Sail reference algorithm.

==== CLSW (RV64)

===== Encoding

CLSW is encoded in the OP-IMM-32 major opcode and is available only in RV64.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 12, name: 'imm=0x603' },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
w = X[rs1][31:0]
c = 0
while (c < 31) & (w >=_s 0xC0000000) & (w <=_s 0x3FFFFFFF) do
    c = c + 1
    w = w << 1
X[rd] = to_bits(XLEN, c)
----

===== Description

CLSW applies the CLS definition to the low 32 bits of `rs1` and writes the count
as an XLEN value.

==== SLX

===== Encoding

SLX is encoded in the OP-32 major opcode.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x3 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0x1, attr: ['SLX'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
shamt = X[rs2][log2(XLEN)-1:0]
X[rd] = ((X[rd] @ X[rs1]) << shamt)[(2*XLEN-1):XLEN]
----

===== Description

SLX shifts the 2*XLEN-bit concatenation `X[rd] @ X[rs1]` left by `shamt` and
writes the upper XLEN bits to `rd`.

==== SRX

===== Encoding

SRX is encoded in the OP-32 major opcode.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x3 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0x5, attr: ['SRX'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
shamt = X[rs2][log2(XLEN)-1:0]
X[rd] = ((X[rs1] @ X[rd]) >> shamt)[(XLEN-1):0]
----

===== Description

SRX shifts the 2*XLEN-bit concatenation `X[rs1] @ X[rd]` right by `shamt` and
writes the lower XLEN bits to `rd`.

==== MVM

===== Encoding

MVM is encoded in the OP-32 major opcode.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0x5, attr: ['MVM'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
m = X[rs2]
X[rd] = (~m & X[rd]) | (m & X[rs1])
----

===== Description

MVM merges `rs1` and the prior value of `rd` under control of the mask `rs2`.

==== MVMN

===== Encoding

MVMN is encoded in the OP-32 major opcode.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0x5, attr: ['MVMN'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
m = X[rs2]
X[rd] = (~m & X[rs1]) | (m & X[rd])
----

===== Description

MVMN is like MVM, but swaps the roles of `rs1` and the prior `rd` value.

==== MERGE

===== Encoding

MERGE is encoded in the OP-32 major opcode.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x3b, attr: ['OP-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0x5, attr: ['MERGE'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
d0 = X[rd]
X[rd] = (~d0 & X[rs1]) | (d0 & X[rs2])
----

===== Description

MERGE uses the prior value of `rd` as the mask to select between `rs1` and `rs2`.

=== Widening Add/Subtract

==== PWADD.B (RV32)

===== Encoding

PWADD.B is available only in RV32. It writes a 64-bit result to an even-odd
register pair specified by `rd_p`.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rd_p' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0x0, attr: ['PWADD.B'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]

for i = 0 .. 3:
    a = s1[(8*i+7):(8*i)]
    b = s2[(8*i+7):(8*i)]
    d[(16*i+15):(16*i)] = to_bits(16, signed(a) + signed(b))

if (rd_p != 0):
    X[2*rd_p]   = d[31:0]
    X[2*rd_p+1] = d[63:32]
----

===== Description

PWADD.B sign-extends corresponding packed 8-bit elements of `rs1` and `rs2` to
signed values, adds them, and produces four packed 16-bit results. The 64-bit
result is written to the register pair `{X[2*rd_p+1], X[2*rd_p]}` when `rd_p != 0`.

==== PWADDA.B (RV32)

===== Encoding

PWADDA.B is available only in RV32. It accumulates into the destination register pair.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rd_p' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0x1, attr: ['PWADDA.B'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]

d = (rd_p == 0) ? 0 : (X[2*rd_p+1] @ X[2*rd_p])

for i = 0 .. 3:
    a = s1[(8*i+7):(8*i)]
    b = s2[(8*i+7):(8*i)]
    acc = d[(16*i+15):(16*i)]
    d[(16*i+15):(16*i)] = acc + to_bits(16, signed(a) + signed(b))

if (rd_p != 0):
    X[2*rd_p]   = d[31:0]
    X[2*rd_p+1] = d[63:32]
----

===== Description

PWADDA.B performs the same packed byte-to-halfword signed additions as PWADD.B,
then adds each 16-bit result into the corresponding 16-bit element of the
destination register pair.

==== PWADDU.B (RV32)

===== Encoding

PWADDU.B is available only in RV32. It writes a 64-bit result to an even-odd
register pair specified by `rd_p`.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rd_p' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0x2, attr: ['PWADDU.B'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]

for i = 0 .. 3:
    a = s1[(8*i+7):(8*i)]
    b = s2[(8*i+7):(8*i)]
    d[(16*i+15):(16*i)] = to_bits(16, unsigned(a) + unsigned(b))

if (rd_p != 0):
    X[2*rd_p]   = d[31:0]
    X[2*rd_p+1] = d[63:32]
----

===== Description

PWADDU.B zero-extends corresponding packed 8-bit elements of `rs1` and `rs2` to
unsigned values, adds them, and produces four packed 16-bit results, written to
the destination register pair when `rd_p != 0`.

==== PWADDAU.B (RV32)

===== Encoding

PWADDAU.B is available only in RV32. It accumulates into the destination register pair.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rd_p' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },

    { bits: 2, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0x3, attr: ['PWADDAU.B'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]

d = (rd_p == 0) ? 0 : (X[2*rd_p+1] @ X[2*rd_p])

for i = 0 .. 3:
    a = s1[(8*i+7):(8*i)]
    b = s2[(8*i+7):(8*i)]
    acc = d[(16*i+15):(16*i)]
    d[(16*i+15):(16*i)] = acc + to_bits(16, unsigned(a) + unsigned(b))

if (rd_p != 0):
    X[2*rd_p]   = d[31:0]
    X[2*rd_p+1] = d[63:32]
----

===== Description

PWADDAU.B performs the same packed byte-to-halfword unsigned additions as PWADDU.B,
then adds each 16-bit result into the corresponding 16-bit element of the
destination register pair.

==== PWSUB.B (RV32)

===== Encoding

PWSUB.B is available only in RV32. It writes a 64-bit result to an even-odd
register pair specified by `rd_p`.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rd_p' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0x8, attr: ['PWSUB.B'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]

for i = 0 .. 3:
    a = s1[(8*i+7):(8*i)]
    b = s2[(8*i+7):(8*i)]
    d[(16*i+15):(16*i)] = to_bits(16, signed(a) - signed(b))

if (rd_p != 0):
    X[2*rd_p]   = d[31:0]
    X[2*rd_p+1] = d[63:32]
----

===== Description

PWSUB.B sign-extends corresponding packed 8-bit elements of `rs1` and `rs2`,
subtracts them, and produces four packed 16-bit results. When `rd_p != 0`,
the 64-bit result is written to the destination register pair
`{X[2*rd_p+1], X[2*rd_p]}`.

==== PWSUBA.B (RV32)

===== Encoding

PWSUBA.B is available only in RV32 and accumulates into the destination
register pair.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rd_p' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0x9, attr: ['PWSUBA.B'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]

d = (rd_p == 0) ? 0 : (X[2*rd_p+1] @ X[2*rd_p])

for i = 0 .. 3:
    a   = s1[(8*i+7):(8*i)]
    b   = s2[(8*i+7):(8*i)]
    acc = d[(16*i+15):(16*i)]
    d[(16*i+15):(16*i)] = acc + to_bits(16, signed(a) - signed(b))

if (rd_p != 0):
    X[2*rd_p]   = d[31:0]
    X[2*rd_p+1] = d[63:32]
----

===== Description

PWSUBA.B performs the same packed byte-to-halfword signed subtraction as
PWSUB.B, then adds each 16-bit result into the corresponding 16-bit element
of the destination register pair.

==== PWADD.H (RV32)

===== Encoding

PWADD.H is available only in RV32. It writes results to an even-odd register
pair specified by `rd_p`.
:contentReference[oaicite:3]{index=3}

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rd_p' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0x0, attr: ['PWADD.H'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]
d0 = to_bits(32, signed(s1[15:0])  + signed(s2[15:0]))
d1 = to_bits(32, signed(s1[31:16]) + signed(s2[31:16]))

if (rd_p != 0):
    X[2*rd_p]   = d0
    X[2*rd_p+1] = d1
----

===== Description

PWADD.H sign-extends each 16-bit halfword element of `rs1` and `rs2`, adds them,
and writes two 32-bit results to the destination register pair when `rd_p != 0`.

==== PWADDA.H (RV32)

===== Encoding

PWADDA.H is available only in RV32 and accumulates into the destination register pair.
:contentReference[oaicite:4]{index=4}

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rd_p' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0x1, attr: ['PWADDA.H'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]

acc0 = X[2*rd_p]
acc1 = (rd_p == 0) ? 0 : X[2*rd_p+1]

acc0 = acc0 + to_bits(32, signed(s1[15:0])  + signed(s2[15:0]))
acc1 = acc1 + to_bits(32, signed(s1[31:16]) + signed(s2[31:16]))

if (rd_p != 0):
    X[2*rd_p]   = acc0
    X[2*rd_p+1] = acc1
----

===== Description

PWADDA.H performs PWADD.H and adds each 32-bit result into the corresponding
32-bit element of the destination register pair.

    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]

acc0 = X[2*rd_p]
acc1 = (rd_p == 0) ? 0 : X[2*rd_p+1]

acc0 = acc0 + to_bits(32, unsigned(s1[15:0])  - unsigned(s2[15:0]))
acc1 = acc1 + to_bits(32, unsigned(s1[31:16]) - unsigned(s2[31:16]))

if (rd_p != 0):
    X[2*rd_p]   = acc0
    X[2*rd_p+1] = acc1
----

===== Description

PWSUBAU.H performs PWSUBU.H and accumulates the two 32-bit results into the
destination register pair.

==== WADD (RV32)

===== Encoding

WADD is available only in RV32 and writes a 64-bit result to register pair `rd_p`.
:contentReference[oaicite:16]{index=16}

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rd_p' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0x0, attr: ['WADD'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
d = to_bits(64, signed(X[rs1]) + signed(X[rs2]))

if (rd_p != 0):
    X[2*rd_p]   = d[31:0]
    X[2*rd_p+1] = d[63:32]
----

===== Description

WADD adds `rs1` and `rs2` as signed XLEN values and writes the 64-bit sum to the
destination register pair when `rd_p != 0`.

==== WADDA (RV32)

===== Encoding

WADDA is available only in RV32 and accumulates into the destination register pair.
:contentReference[oaicite:17]{index=17}

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rd_p' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0x1, attr: ['WADDA'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
acc = (rd_p == 0) ? 0 : (X[2*rd_p+1] @ X[2*rd_p])
acc = acc + to_bits(64, signed(X[rs1]) + signed(X[rs2]))

if (rd_p != 0):
    X[2*rd_p]   = acc[31:0]
    X[2*rd_p+1] = acc[63:32]
----

===== Description

WADDA performs WADD and accumulates the 64-bit result into the destination
register pair.

==== WSUB (RV32)

===== Encoding

WSUB is available only in RV32.
:contentReference[oaicite:20]{index=20}

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rd_p' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 0x8, attr: ['WSUB'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
d = to_bits(64, signed(X[rs1]) - signed(X[rs2]))

if (rd_p != 0):
    X[2*rd_p]   = d[31:0]
    X[2*rd_p+1] = d[63:32]
----

===== Description

WSUB subtracts `rs2` from `rs1` as signed XLEN values and writes the 64-bit
difference to the destination register pair when `rd_p != 0`.

=== Widening Shift

==== PWSLLI.B (RV32)

===== Encoding

PWSLLI.B is available only in RV32. The shift amount is encoded in the `w_uimm`
field (element width plus immediate). The destination is a register pair `rd_p`.
:contentReference[oaicite:3]{index=3}

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rd_p' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 7, name: 'w_uimm' },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x0, attr: ['PWSLLI.B'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1    = X[rs1]
shamt = w_uimm[3:0]

for i = 0 .. 3:
    a = s1[(8*i+7):(8*i)]
    d[(16*i+15):(16*i)] = zero_extend(16, a) << shamt

if (rd_p != 0):
    X[2*rd_p]   = d[31:0]
    X[2*rd_p+1] = d[63:32]
----

===== Description

PWSLLI.B widens each 8-bit element of `rs1` to 16 bits by zero-extension, then
shifts left by an immediate amount, producing four 16-bit results.

==== PWSLL.BS (RV32)

===== Encoding

PWSLL.BS is available only in RV32. The shift amount is taken from `rs2`.
:contentReference[oaicite:4]{index=4}

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rd_p' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x0, attr: ['PWSLL.BS'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1    = X[rs1]
shamt = X[rs2][4:0]

for i = 0 .. 3:
    a = s1[(8*i+7):(8*i)]
    d[(16*i+15):(16*i)] = (zero_extend(32, a) << shamt)[15:0]

if (rd_p != 0):
    X[2*rd_p]   = d[31:0]
    X[2*rd_p+1] = d[63:32]
----

===== Description

PWSLL.BS widens each 8-bit element of `rs1` to 16 bits by zero-extension, then
shifts left by the amount in `rs2` (low 5 bits), producing four 16-bit results.

d = sign_extend(64, X[rs1]) << shamt

if (rd_p != 0):
    X[2*rd_p]   = d[31:0]
    X[2*rd_p+1] = d[63:32]
----

===== Description

WSLAI sign-extends `rs1` to 64 bits, shifts left by an immediate amount, and
writes the 64-bit result to the destination register pair when `rd_p != 0`.


=== Widening Zip

==== WZIP8P (RV32)

===== Encoding

WZIP8P is available only in RV32. It writes its 64-bit result to the even-odd
register pair specified by `rd_p` (no write occurs if `rd_p = 0`).
It is encoded in the RV32 register-pair OP-IMM-32 format with `f=111` and `w=10`.
:contentReference[oaicite:1]{index=1}

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rd_p' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x7, attr: ['WZIP8P'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]

lo = s2[15:8]  @ s1[15:8]  @ s2[7:0]   @ s1[7:0]
hi = s2[31:24] @ s1[31:24] @ s2[23:16] @ s1[23:16]

if (rd_p != 0):
    X[2*rd_p]   = lo
    X[2*rd_p+1] = hi
----

===== Description

WZIP8P interleaves the low four bytes of `rs1` and `rs2` into a 64-bit result,
arranged as two 32-bit halves. The lower destination register receives the
interleaving of bytes [15:0], and the upper destination register receives the
interleaving of bytes [31:16].

==== WZIP16P (RV32)

===== Encoding

WZIP16P is available only in RV32. It writes its 64-bit result to the even-odd
register pair specified by `rd_p` (no write occurs if `rd_p = 0`).
It is encoded in the RV32 register-pair OP-IMM-32 format with `f=111` and `w=11`.
:contentReference[oaicite:2]{index=2}

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rd_p' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x2 },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs1' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x3 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x7, attr: ['WZIP16P'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = X[rs1]
s2 = X[rs2]

lo = s2[15:0]  @ s1[15:0]
hi = s2[31:16] @ s1[31:16]

if (rd_p != 0):
    X[2*rd_p]   = lo
    X[2*rd_p+1] = hi
----

===== Description

WZIP16P interleaves 16-bit halfwords from `rs1` and `rs2` into a 64-bit result.
The lower destination register receives `{rs2[15:0], rs1[15:0]}`, and the upper
destination register receives `{rs2[31:16], rs1[31:16]}`.


=== Reduction Sum (double-wide)

==== PREDSUM.DBS (RV32)

===== Encoding

PREDSUM.DBS is available only in RV32. It reads a 64-bit packed source from the
even-odd register pair specified by `rs1_p` and produces a 32-bit scalar result
in `rd`. If `rs1_p = 0`, the source pair is treated as zero.

PREDSUM.DBS is encoded in the OP-IMM-32 major opcode with `func3=100`, bit 28
set to 1, and `rs1_p` selecting the source register pair.
:contentReference[oaicite:2]{index=2}

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x4 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1_p' },
    { bits: 6, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x1, attr: ['PREDSUM.DBS'] },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 =
  (rs1_p == 0) ? 0
               : (X[2*rs1_p+1] @ X[2*rs1_p])      // 64-bit

sum = signed(X[rs2])                              // scalar accumulator (int)

for i = 0 .. 7:
    sum += signed(s1[(8*i+7) : (8*i)])            // signed bytes

X[rd] = to_bits(32, sum)
----

===== Description

PREDSUM.DBS adds the eight signed 8-bit elements contained in the 64-bit source
register pair `rs1_p` to the signed scalar value in `rs2`, and writes the low
32 bits of the resulting sum to `rd`.

==== PREDSUMU.DBS (RV32)

===== Encoding

PREDSUMU.DBS is available only in RV32. It reads a 64-bit packed source from the
even-odd register pair specified by `rs1_p` and produces a 32-bit scalar result
in `rd`. If `rs1_p = 0`, the source pair is treated as zero.
:contentReference[oaicite:3]{index=3}

[wavedrom, ,svg]

{reg:[

    { bits: 3, name: 0x4 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1_p' },
    { bits: 6, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x3, attr: ['PREDSUMU.DBS'] },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 =
  (rs1_p == 0) ? 0
               : (X[2*rs1_p+1] @ X[2*rs1_p])      // 64-bit

for i = 0 .. 7:
    sum += unsigned(s1[(8*i+7) : (8*i)])          // unsigned bytes

X[rd] = to_bits(32, sum)
----

===== Description

PREDSUMU.DBS adds the eight unsigned 8-bit elements contained in the 64-bit
source register pair `rs1_p` to the unsigned scalar value in `rs2`, and writes
the low 32 bits of the resulting sum to `rd`.

==== PREDSUM.DHS (RV32)

===== Encoding

PREDSUM.DHS is available only in RV32. It reads a 64-bit packed source from the

:contentReference[oaicite:4]{index=4}

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[

    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x4 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1_p' },
    { bits: 6, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x1, attr: ['PREDSUM.DHS'] },

....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 =
  (rs1_p == 0) ? 0
               : (X[2*rs1_p+1] @ X[2*rs1_p])      // 64-bit

sum = signed(X[rs2])                              // scalar accumulator (int)

for i = 0 .. 3:
    sum += signed(s1[(16*i+15) : (16*i)])         // signed halfwords

X[rd] = to_bits(32, sum)
----

===== Description

PREDSUM.DHS adds the four signed 16-bit elements contained in the 64-bit source
register pair `rs1_p` to the signed scalar value in `rs2`, and writes the low
32 bits of the resulting sum to `rd`.

==== PREDSUMU.DHS (RV32)

===== Encoding

PREDSUMU.DHS is available only in RV32. It reads a 64-bit packed source from the
even-odd register pair specified by `rs1_p` and produces a 32-bit scalar result
in `rd`. If `rs1_p = 0`, the source pair is treated as zero.
:contentReference[oaicite:5]{index=5}

[wavedrom, ,svg]

    { bits: 3, name: 0x4 },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1_p' },
    { bits: 6, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 =
  (rs1_p == 0) ? 0
               : (X[2*rs1_p+1] @ X[2*rs1_p])      // 64-bit

sum = unsigned(X[rs2])                            // scalar accumulator (int)

for i = 0 .. 3:
    sum += unsigned(s1[(16*i+15) : (16*i)])       // unsigned halfwords

X[rd] = to_bits(32, sum)
----

===== Description

PREDSUMU.DHS adds the four unsigned 16-bit elements contained in the 64-bit
source register pair `rs1_p` to the unsigned scalar value in `rs2`, and writes
the low 32 bits of the resulting sum to `rd`.


=== Narrowing Shift

==== PNSRLI.B (RV32)

===== Encoding

PNSRLI.B is encoded using the OP-IMM-32 major opcode. It reads a 64-bit source
from the register pair selected by `rs1p` and produces a packed byte result in
`rd`.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xc },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1p' },
    { bits: 7, name: 'w-uimm' },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x0, attr: ['PNSRLI.B'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

`w-uimm[6:4]` selects the element width and must be `001` for the `.B` form.
`w-uimm[3:0]` provides the 4-bit shift amount.

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = (rs1p == 0) ? 0 : (X[2*rs1p+1] @ X[2*rs1p])
shamt = w_uimm[3:0]

for i = 0 .. 3:
    h = s1[(16*i+15):(16*i)]                 // 16-bit lane
    d[(8*i+7):(8*i)] = (zext_32(h) >> shamt)[7:0]

X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

PNSRLI.B extracts four 16-bit lanes from a 64-bit register-pair source, performs
a logical right shift by an immediate amount, and packs the low byte of each
shifted lane into `rd`.

==== PNSRL.BS (RV32)

===== Encoding

PNSRL.BS is encoded using the OP-IMM-32 major opcode. It reads a 64-bit source
from `rs1p` and uses `rs2[4:0]` as the shift amount.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xc },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1p' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x0, attr: ['PNSRL.BS'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = (rs1p == 0) ? 0 : (X[2*rs1p+1] @ X[2*rs1p])
shamt = X[rs2][4:0]

for i = 0 .. 3:
    h = s1[(16*i+15):(16*i)]
    d[(8*i+7):(8*i)] = (zext_32(h) >> shamt)[7:0]

X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

PNSRL.BS performs a per-lane logical right shift of four 16-bit lanes taken from
a 64-bit register-pair source, using a shift amount from `rs2`. The low byte of
each shifted lane is packed into `rd`.

==== PNSRAI.B (RV32)

===== Encoding

PNSRAI.B is encoded using the OP-IMM-32 major opcode. It reads a 64-bit source
from the register pair selected by `rs1p` and produces a packed byte result in
`rd`.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xc },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1p' },
    { bits: 7, name: 'w-uimm' },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x4, attr: ['PNSRAI.B'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

`w-uimm[6:4]` must be `001` for the `.B` form and `w-uimm[3:0]` is the shift
amount.

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = (rs1p == 0) ? 0 : (X[2*rs1p+1] @ X[2*rs1p])
shamt = w_uimm[3:0]

for i = 0 .. 3:
    h = s1[(16*i+15):(16*i)]
    d[(8*i+7):(8*i)] = (sext_32(h) >> shamt)[7:0]

X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

PNSRAI.B extracts four 16-bit lanes from a 64-bit register-pair source, performs
an arithmetic right shift by an immediate amount, and packs the low byte of each
shifted lane into `rd`.

==== PNSRA.BS (RV32)

===== Encoding

PNSRA.BS is encoded using the OP-IMM-32 major opcode. It reads a 64-bit source
from `rs1p` and uses `rs2[4:0]` as the shift amount.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xc },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1p' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x4, attr: ['PNSRA.BS'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

[source,pseudocode]

s1 = (rs1p == 0) ? 0 : (X[2*rs1p+1] @ X[2*rs1p])
shamt = X[rs2][4:0]

for i = 0 .. 3:
    h = s1[(16*i+15):(16*i)]
    d[(8*i+7):(8*i)] = (sext_32(h) >> shamt)[7:0]

X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

PNSRA.BS performs a per-lane arithmetic right shift of four 16-bit lanes taken
from a 64-bit register-pair source, using a shift amount from `rs2`. The low
byte of each shifted lane is packed into `rd`.

==== PNSRARI.B (RV32)

===== Encoding

PNSRARI.B is encoded using the OP-IMM-32 major opcode. It reads a 64-bit source
from `rs1p` and performs a rounded arithmetic right shift by an immediate amount.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xc },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1p' },
    { bits: 7, name: 'w-uimm' },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x5, attr: ['PNSRARI.B'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

`w-uimm[6:4]` must be `001` for the `.B` form and `w-uimm[3:0]` is the shift
amount.

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = (rs1p == 0) ? 0 : (X[2*rs1p+1] @ X[2*rs1p])
shamt = w_uimm[3:0]

for i = 0 .. 3:
    h  = s1[(16*i+15):(16*i)]
    // Compute rounded arithmetic shift: ( (h << 1) >> shamt + 1 ) >> 1
    shx = ((sext_32(h) @ 0b0) >> shamt)[8:0]
    d[(8*i+7):(8*i)] = (shx + 1)[8:1]

X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

PNSRARI.B performs a per-lane rounded arithmetic right shift of four 16-bit lanes
from a 64-bit register-pair source using an immediate shift amount, and packs
the resulting bytes into `rd`.

==== PNSRAR.BS (RV32)

===== Encoding

PNSRAR.BS is encoded using the OP-IMM-32 major opcode. It reads a 64-bit source
from `rs1p` and uses `rs2[4:0]` as the shift amount.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xc },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1p' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x5, attr: ['PNSRAR.BS'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1 = (rs1p == 0) ? 0 : (X[2*rs1p+1] @ X[2*rs1p])
shamt = X[rs2][4:0]

for i = 0 .. 3:
    h  = s1[(16*i+15):(16*i)]
    shx = ((sext_32(h) @ 0b0) >> shamt)[8:0]
    d[(8*i+7):(8*i)] = (shx + 1)[8:1]

X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

PNSRAR.BS performs a per-lane rounded arithmetic right shift of four 16-bit lanes
from a 64-bit register-pair source using a shift amount from `rs2`, and packs
the resulting bytes into `rd`.

==== PNSRLI.H (RV32)

===== Encoding

PNSRLI.H is encoded using the OP-IMM-32 major opcode. It reads a 64-bit source
from `rs1p`, shifts each 32-bit word lane right by an immediate amount, and packs
the low 16 bits of each shifted word into `rd`.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xc },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1p' },
    { bits: 7, name: 'w-uimm' },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x0, attr: ['PNSRLI.H'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

`w-uimm[6:5]` selects the `.H` form and `w-uimm[4:0]` provides the 5-bit shift
amount.

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1    = (rs1p == 0) ? 0 : (X[2*rs1p+1] @ X[2*rs1p])
shamt = w_uimm[4:0]

d[15:0]  = (s1[31:0]  >> shamt)[15:0]
d[31:16] = (s1[63:32] >> shamt)[15:0]

X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

PNSRLI.H performs a logical right shift of each 32-bit word lane in a 64-bit
register-pair source by an immediate amount, then packs the low 16 bits of each
shifted word into `rd`.

==== PNSRL.HS (RV32)

===== Encoding

PNSRL.HS is encoded using the OP-IMM-32 major opcode. It reads a 64-bit source
from `rs1p`, uses `rs2[4:0]` as the shift amount, and packs 16-bit results into
`rd`.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xc },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1p' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x0, attr: ['PNSRL.HS'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1    = (rs1p == 0) ? 0 : (X[2*rs1p+1] @ X[2*rs1p])
shamt = X[rs2][4:0]

d[15:0]  = (s1[31:0]  >> shamt)[15:0]
d[31:16] = (s1[63:32] >> shamt)[15:0]

X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

PNSRL.HS performs a logical right shift of each 32-bit word lane in a 64-bit
register-pair source by a shift amount from `rs2`, then packs the low 16 bits of
each shifted word into `rd`.

==== PNSRAI.H (RV32)

===== Encoding

PNSRAI.H is encoded using the OP-IMM-32 major opcode. It reads a 64-bit source
from `rs1p`, performs an arithmetic right shift by an immediate amount on each
32-bit word lane, and packs 16-bit results into `rd`.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xc },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1p' },
    { bits: 7, name: 'w-uimm' },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x4, attr: ['PNSRAI.H'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

`w-uimm` selects the `.H` form and provides a 5-bit shift amount (`w_uimm[4:0]`).

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1    = (rs1p == 0) ? 0 : (X[2*rs1p+1] @ X[2*rs1p])
shamt = w_uimm[4:0]

d[15:0]  = (sext_48(s1[31:0])  >> shamt)[15:0]
d[31:16] = (sext_48(s1[63:32]) >> shamt)[15:0]

X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

PNSRAI.H performs an arithmetic right shift of each 32-bit word lane in a 64-bit
register-pair source by an immediate amount, then packs the low 16 bits of each
shifted word into `rd`.

==== PNSRA.HS (RV32)

===== Encoding

PNSRA.HS is encoded using the OP-IMM-32 major opcode. It reads a 64-bit source
from `rs1p`, uses `rs2[4:0]` as the shift amount, performs per-word arithmetic
right shifts, and packs 16-bit results into `rd`.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xc },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1p' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x4, attr: ['PNSRA.HS'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1    = (rs1p == 0) ? 0 : (X[2*rs1p+1] @ X[2*rs1p])
shamt = X[rs2][4:0]

d[15:0]  = (sext_48(s1[31:0])  >> shamt)[15:0]
d[31:16] = (sext_48(s1[63:32]) >> shamt)[15:0]

X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

PNSRA.HS performs an arithmetic right shift of each 32-bit word lane in a 64-bit
register-pair source by a shift amount from `rs2`, then packs the low 16 bits of
each shifted word into `rd`.

==== PNSRARI.H (RV32)

===== Encoding

PNSRARI.H is encoded using the OP-IMM-32 major opcode. It performs a per-word
*rounded* arithmetic right shift by an immediate amount and packs 16-bit results
into `rd`.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xc },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1p' },
    { bits: 7, name: 'w-uimm' },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x5, attr: ['PNSRARI.H'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1    = (rs1p == 0) ? 0 : (X[2*rs1p+1] @ X[2*rs1p])
shamt = w_uimm[4:0]

for i = 0 .. 1:
    w   = s1[(32*i+31):(32*i)]
    shx = ((sext_48(w) @ 0b0) >> shamt)[16:0]
    d[(16*i+15):(16*i)] = (shx + 1)[16:1]

X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

PNSRARI.H performs a per-word *rounded* arithmetic right shift of the 64-bit
register-pair source by an immediate amount. The low 16 bits of each rounded
shifted word are packed into `rd`.

==== PNSRAR.HS (RV32)

===== Encoding

PNSRAR.HS is encoded using the OP-IMM-32 major opcode. It performs a per-word
*rounded* arithmetic right shift using `rs2[4:0]` as the shift amount.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xc },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1p' },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },
    { bits: 2, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x5, attr: ['PNSRAR.HS'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1    = (rs1p == 0) ? 0 : (X[2*rs1p+1] @ X[2*rs1p])
shamt = X[rs2][4:0]

for i = 0 .. 1:
    w   = s1[(32*i+31):(32*i)]
    shx = ((sext_48(w) @ 0b0) >> shamt)[16:0]
    d[(16*i+15):(16*i)] = (shx + 1)[16:1]

X[rd] = d
----

===== Description

PNSRAR.HS performs a per-word *rounded* arithmetic right shift of a 64-bit
register-pair source using a shift amount from `rs2`, and packs 16-bit results
into `rd`.

==== NSRLI (RV32)

===== Encoding

NSRLI is encoded using the OP-IMM-32 major opcode. It reads a 64-bit register-pair
source from `rs1p`, performs a logical right shift by an immediate amount, and
writes the low 32 bits to `rd`.

[wavedrom, ,svg]
....
{reg:[
    { bits: 7, name: 0x1b, attr: ['OP-IMM-32'] },
    { bits: 5, name: 'rd' },
    { bits: 4, name: 0xc },
    { bits: 4, name: 'rs1p' },
    { bits: 7, name: 'w-uimm' },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x0, attr: ['NSRLI'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}
....

For NSRLI, `w-uimm` uses the `1xxxxxx` encoding class and `w_uimm[5:0]` is the
shift amount.

===== Operation

[source,pseudocode]
----
s1    = (rs1p == 0) ? 0 : (X[2*rs1p+1] @ X[2*rs1p])
shamt = w_uimm[5:0]
X[rd] = (s1 >> shamt)[31:0]
----

===== Description

NSRLI performs a 64-bit logical right shift of the register-pair source by an
immediate amount and returns the low 32 bits.

==== NSRL (RV32)

amount.

[wavedrom, ,svg]

    { bits: 5, name: 'rs2' },

    { bits: 1, name: 0x1 },
    { bits: 3, name: 0x0, attr: ['NSRL'] },
    { bits: 1, name: 0x0 },
]}

----

===== Description
